    function ShowHide(SwitchID, OpenID, CloseID) {
      var vobj;
      if (SwitchID > '') {
        vobj = document.getElementById(SwitchID);
        if (vobj.style.display == '') {
          vobj.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
          vobj.style.display = '';
        }
      }
      if (OpenID > '') {
        vobj = document.getElementById(OpenID);
        vobj.style.display = '';
      }
      if (CloseID > '') {
        vobj = document.getElementById(CloseID);
        vobj.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  </script>

      function change_star(s_index) {
        if (GetCookie("nownews_horoscope_month_cookies") != null) {
          $("#star").html(luck[GetCookie("nownews_horoscope_month_cookies")]);
          $("#star_url").attr("href", urls[GetCookie("nownews_horoscope_month_cookies")]);
        } else {
          $("#star").html(luck[s_index]);
          $("#star_url").attr("href", urls[s_index]);
        }
      }
      change_star(Math.ceil(Math.random() * 11));

      function click_horoscope(horoscope_month) {
        ClearCookie('nownews_horoscope_month_cookies');
        SetCookie('nownews_horoscope_month_cookies', horoscope_month, '999', '/', 'nownews.com');
        $("#star").html(luck[horoscope_month]);
        $("#star_url").attr("href", urls[horoscope_month]);
        window.open(urls[horoscope_month], '_blank', '');
        ShowHide('', '', 'horoscopes');
      }

      function GetCookie(name) {
        var result = null;
        var myCookie = document.cookie + ";";
        var searchName = name + "=";
        var startOfCookie = myCookie.indexOf(searchName);
        var endOfCookie;
        if (startOfCookie != -1) {
          startOfCookie += searchName.length;
          endOfCookie = myCookie.indexOf(";", startOfCookie);
          result = unescape(myCookie.substring(startOfCookie, endOfCookie));
        }
        return result;
      }

      function SetCookie(name, value, expires, path, domain, secure) {
        var expDays = expires * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
        var expDate = new Date();
        expDate.setTime(expDate.getTime() + expDays);
        var expString = ((expires == null) ? "" : (";expires=" + expDate.toGMTString()))
        var pathString = ((path == null) ? "" : (";path=" + path))
        var domainString = ((domain == null) ? "" : (";domain=" + domain))
        var secureString = ((secure == true) ? ";secure" : "")
        document.cookie = name + "=" + escape(value) + expString + pathString + domainString + secureString;
      }

      function ClearCookie(name) {
        var ThreeDays = 3 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
        var expDate = new Date();
        expDate.setTime(expDate.getTime() - ThreeDays);
        document.cookie = name + "=;expires=" + expDate.toGMTString();
      }
    </script>
